    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    (e.target as Element).setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);

     2 // Shows key concepts, an animated diagram, and interactive controls relevant to the topic.
     3 import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
     4 import { getExperiment } from '@/lib/experiments';
     5 
     6 interface Props {
     7   experimentId: string;
     8   onEvent: (e: string) => void;
     9 }
    10

    12 interface Config {
    13   bg: string;
    14   accent: string;
    15   concepts: string[];
    16   controls: { label: string; action: string }[];
    17   drawFrame: (ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, w: number, h: number, t: number, state: number) => void;
    18 }

    20 function defaultDraw(accent: string) {
    21   return (ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, w: number, h: number, t: number, state: number) => {
    22     ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
    23     // Animated particle field
    24     const count = 18 + state * 4;
    25     for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    26       const angle = (i / count) * Math.PI * 2 + t * 0.003;
    27       const r = 60 + Math.sin(t * 0.02 + i) * 25;
    28       const x = w / 2 + r * Math.cos(angle);
    29       const y = h / 2 + r * Math.sin(angle) * 0.55;
    30       ctx.beginPath();
    31       ctx.arc(x, y, 5 + Math.sin(t * 0.04 + i) * 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    32       ctx.fillStyle = accent + 'CC';
    33       ctx.fill();
    34     }
    35     // Central glow
    36     const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(w / 2, h / 2, 0, w / 2, h / 2, 50);
    37     g.addColorStop(0, accent + '44');
    38     g.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
    39     ctx.fillStyle = g;
    40     ctx.beginPath();
    41     ctx.arc(w / 2, h / 2, 50, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    42     ctx.fill();
    43   };
    44 }

   317 export default function GenericLabCanvas({ experimentId, onEvent }: Props) {
   318   const experiment = getExperiment(experimentId);
   319   const cfg = getConfig(experimentId);
   320   const canvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);
   321   const rafRef = useRef<number>(0);
   322   const [simState, setSimState] = useState(0);
   323   const [log, setLog] = useState<string[]>([]);
   324 
   325   useEffect(() => {
   326     const canvas = canvasRef.current;
   327     if (!canvas) return;
   328     const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
   329     if (!ctx) return;
   330     let frame = 0;
   331     function tick() {
   332       ctx!.clearRect(0, 0, canvas!.width, canvas!.height);
   333       cfg.drawFrame(ctx!, canvas!.width, canvas!.height, frame, simState);
   334       frame++;
   335       rafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   336     }
   337     tick();

     9 // ── Animated hero canvas: orbiting molecules ──────────────────────────
    10 function HeroCanvas() {
    11   const canvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);
    12   useEffect(() => {
    13     const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    14     if (!canvas) return;
    15     const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d')!;
    16     const W = canvas.width  = 440;
    17     const H = canvas.height = 440;
    18     type Node = { x: number; y: number; r: number; vx: number; vy: number; color: string };
    19     const PALETTE = ['#1B4332','#2D6A4F','#52796F','#F59E0B','#84A98C','#D97706'];
    20     const nodes: Node[] = [
    21       { x:220,y:220,r:22,vx: 0.22,vy: 0.15,color:'#1B4332' },
    22       { x:130,y:150,r:15,vx:-0.16,vy: 0.26,color:'#2D6A4F' },
    23       { x:320,y:140,r:13,vx: 0.26,vy:-0.19,color:'#F59E0B' },
    24       { x:335,y:300,r:16,vx:-0.21,vy:-0.21,color:'#52796F' },
    25       { x:115,y:305,r:12,vx: 0.19,vy:-0.26,color:'#84A98C' },
    26       { x:220,y: 90,r:10,vx:-0.23,vy: 0.21,color:'#2D6A4F' },
    27       { x:375,y:220,r:11,vx:-0.19,vy: 0.23,color:'#1B4332' },
    28       { x: 60,y:220,r:11,vx: 0.23,vy:-0.16,color:'#F59E0B' },
    29       { x:220,y:350,r:10,vx: 0.16,vy: 0.21,color:'#52796F' },
    30     ];
    31     const bonds = [{a:0,b:1},{a:0,b:2},{a:0,b:3},{a:0,b:4},{a:1,b:5},{a:2,b:6},{a:3,b:7},{a:4,b:8},{a:5,b:6},{a:6,b:3},{a:1,b:4}];
    32     let frame = 0, raf: number;
    33     function draw() {
    34       ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);
    35       // Glow bg
    36       const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2,H/2,20,W/2,H/2,180);
    37       grad.addColorStop(0,'rgba(27,67,50,0.07)'); grad.addColorStop(1,'transparent');
    38       ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
    39       // Bonds
    40       bonds.forEach(b => {
    41         const na=nodes[b.a],nb=nodes[b.b];
    42         ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(na.x,na.y); ctx.lineTo(nb.x,nb.y);
    43         ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(27,67,50,0.14)'; ctx.lineWidth=2.5; ctx.stroke();
    44       });
    45       // Nodes
    46       nodes.forEach((n,i) => {
    47         const pulse = 1 + 0.07*Math.sin(frame*0.033+i);
    48         // Outer glow
    49         const g = ctx.createRadialGradient(n.x,n.y,0,n.x,n.y,n.r*pulse*1.6);
    50         g.addColorStop(0, n.color+'44'); g.addColorStop(1,'transparent');
    51         ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(n.x,n.y,n.r*pulse*1.6,0,Math.PI*2);
    52         ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fill();
    53         // Core
    54         ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(n.x,n.y,n.r*pulse,0,Math.PI*2);
    55         ctx.fillStyle=n.color; ctx.globalAlpha=0.9; ctx.fill();
    56         ctx.globalAlpha=1;
    57         // Highlight
    58         ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(n.x-n.r*0.3,n.y-n.r*0.3,n.r*0.3,0,Math.PI*2);
    59         ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,0.35)'; ctx.fill();
    60         // Drift
    61         n.x += n.vx*Math.sin(frame*0.009+i); n.y += n.vy*Math.cos(frame*0.009+i*0.7);
    62         n.x = Math.max(n.r*2, Math.min(W-n.r*2, n.x));
    63         n.y = Math.max(n.r*2, Math.min(H-n.r*2, n.y));
    64       });
    65       // Orbiting electrons
    66       PALETTE.forEach((col,i) => {
    67         const orbit=155+i*10, speed=0.007+i*0.0015;
    68         const angle=frame*speed+(i*Math.PI*2)/PALETTE.length;
    69         const dx=220+orbit*Math.cos(angle), dy=220+orbit*Math.sin(angle);
    70         ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(dx,dy,3.5,0,Math.PI*2);
    71         ctx.fillStyle=col; ctx.globalAlpha=0.6; ctx.fill(); ctx.globalAlpha=1;
    72       });
    73       // Floating formula labels
    74       const labels = [
    75         {text:'HCl',x:280,y:80},{text:'NaOH',x:100,y:90},{text:'C₆H₁₂O₆',x:350,y:370},
    76         {text:'CO₂',x:60,y:350},{text:'CH₄',x:350,y:175},{text:'H₂O',x:95,y:188},
    77       ];
    78       labels.forEach((l,i) => {
    79         ctx.font='bold 11px Inter,sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign='center';
    80         ctx.fillStyle='rgba(27,67,50,0.35)';
    81         const y = l.y + Math.sin(frame*0.018+i)*4;
    82         ctx.fillText(l.text, l.x, y);
    83       });
    84       frame++; raf=requestAnimationFrame(draw);
    85     }
    86     draw();
    87     return () => cancelAnimationFrame(raf);
    88   }, []);
    89   return <canvas ref={canvasRef} style={{ width:400,height:400,maxWidth:'100%' }}/>;
    90 }

      const cur = searches[Math.min(step, searches.length-1)];

        ctx.beginPath();

  'sorting-algorithms': {
    bg: '#F0F9FF', accent: '#0EA5E9',
    concepts: ['Bubble sort: O(n²) — swaps adjacent pairs', 'Merge sort: O(n log n) — divide & conquer', 'Quick sort: O(n log n) avg — pivot partitioning', 'Counting sort: O(n+k) — non-comparison'],
    controls: [{ label: 'Next Pass', action: 'Bubble sort pass completed — largest element settled' }, { label: 'Reset', action: 'New random array generated — ready to sort' }],
    drawFrame: (ctx, w, h, t) => {
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
      const n = 12;
      const pass = Math.floor(t / 100) % (n - 1);
      const vals = [8, 3, 11, 1, 7, 5, 9, 2, 10, 4, 6, 12];
      // Simulate bubble sort passes
      const arr = [...vals];
      for (let p = 0; p < pass; p++) {
        for (let j = 0; j < n - 1 - p; j++) {
          if (arr[j] > arr[j + 1]) { const tmp = arr[j]; arr[j] = arr[j+1]; arr[j+1] = tmp; }
        }
      }
      const curSwap = Math.floor((t % 100) / 10) % (n - 1 - pass);
      const bw = (w - 40) / n;
      const maxVal = 12;

        if (i === curSwap || i === curSwap + 1) fill = '#F59E0B';
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.roundRect(x + 2, y, bw - 4, barH, [3, 3, 0, 0]);
        ctx.fillStyle = fill; ctx.fill();

        ctx.fillText(String(val), x + bw / 2, h - 28);
      });
      ctx.font = 'bold 11px Inter,sans-serif'; ctx.fillStyle = '#0C4A6E'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.fillText(`Bubble Sort — Pass ${pass + 1}/${n - 1}  |  🟡 swapping  🟢 sorted`, w / 2, 18);
    },
  },

      });

    },

      });

      ctx.fillText(`BFS Visit Order: ${bfsOrder.slice(0, visitStep + 1).join(' → ')}`, w / 2, h - 18);
    },

  'hash-table': {
    bg: '#F0F9FF', accent: '#0EA5E9',

    controls: [{ label: 'Insert Key', action: 'Key hashed → bucket found — O(1) insertion' }, { label: 'Lookup', action: 'Hash computed → direct bucket access — O(1) avg' }],

        {bucket:1, key:'"apple"',   highlight: false},
        {bucket:3, key:'"banana"',  highlight: false},
        {bucket:3, key:'"cherry"',  highlight: true},  // collision chained
        {bucket:5, key:'"date"',    highlight: false},
        {bucket:7, key:'"elderberry"', highlight: false},

        ctx.strokeStyle = '#BAE6FD'; ctx.lineWidth = 1; ctx.stroke();

        ctx.fillText(`[${i}]`, bx - 28, y + 16);
        const slotEntries = entries.filter(e => e.bucket === i);

          ctx.fillStyle = isActive ? '#fff' : '#0C4A6E'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
          ctx.fillText(e.key, ex + 44, y + 15);
          if (j < slotEntries.length - 1) {
            ctx.font = '10px Inter,sans-serif'; ctx.fillStyle = '#F59E0B';
            ctx.fillText('→', ex + 96, y + 15);
          }
        });
      }
      ctx.font = '10px Inter,sans-serif'; ctx.fillStyle = '#F59E0B'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.fillText('🔗 Chaining collision at bucket [3]', w / 2, h - 10);
    },
  },

  'finite-state-machine': {

    controls: [{ label: 'Input "a"', action: 'Transition on "a" — moved to next state' }, { label: 'Input "b"', action: 'Transition on "b" — looping or advancing state' }],

      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
      const step = Math.floor(t / 80) % 4;
      // Simple DFA: accepts strings ending in 'ab'
      const states = [

        {from:2, to:2, label:'b', loop:true},
      ];
      const activeState = [0,1,2,2,1][step];
      // Transitions

        if (tr.loop) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.arc(fs.x, fs.y - 28, 14, Math.PI*0.2, Math.PI*0.8);

        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(fs.x + (tr.from < tr.to ? 20 : -20), fs.y);
        ctx.quadraticCurveTo(mx, my, ts.x + (tr.from < tr.to ? -20 : 20), ts.y);
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#BAE6FD'; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5; ctx.stroke();
        ctx.font = '10px Inter,sans-serif'; ctx.fillStyle = '#0C4A6E'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.fillText(tr.label, mx, my - 4);
      });

      states.forEach((s, i) => {
        const isActive = i === activeState;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(s.x, s.y, 22, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = isActive ? '#0EA5E9' : '#E0F2FE';
        ctx.fill();
        ctx.strokeStyle = isActive ? '#0284C7' : '#7DD3FC'; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
        if (s.accept) {
          ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(s.x, s.y, 17, 0, Math.PI * 2);
          ctx.strokeStyle = isActive ? '#fff' : '#0284C7'; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5; ctx.stroke();
        }
        if (s.start) {
          ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(s.x - 36, s.y); ctx.lineTo(s.x - 22, s.y);
          ctx.strokeStyle = '#0C4A6E'; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5; ctx.stroke();
          ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(s.x - 24, s.y - 4); ctx.lineTo(s.x - 22, s.y); ctx.lineTo(s.x - 24, s.y + 4);
          ctx.stroke();
        }
        ctx.font = `bold 13px Inter,sans-serif`; ctx.fillStyle = isActive ? '#fff' : '#0C4A6E'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
        ctx.fillText(s.label, s.x, s.y + 5);
      });
      const inputSeq = ['ε','a','ab','abb'];
      ctx.font = 'bold 11px Inter,sans-serif'; ctx.fillStyle = '#0C4A6E'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
      ctx.fillText(`DFA — accepts strings ending in "ab"`, w / 2, 18);
      ctx.font = '11px Inter,sans-serif'; ctx.fillStyle = activeState === 2 ? '#10B981' : '#64748B';
      ctx.fillText(`Input: "${inputSeq[step]}" → ${activeState === 2 ? '✅ ACCEPT' : '⏳ processing…'}`, w / 2, h - 14);
    },
  },
};

   117 function findReaction(a: Chemical, b: Chemical): RxnRule | null {
   118   for (const rule of REACTION_RULES) {
   119     const [r1, r2] = rule.ids;
   120     if ((a.id === r1 && b.id === r2) || (a.id === r2 && b.id === r1)) return rule;
   121   }
   122   return null;
   123 }

   125 // ── Colour helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   126 function blendColors(chemicals: VesselChemical[]): string {
   127   if (chemicals.length === 0) return 'rgba(180,220,255,0.25)';
   128   if (chemicals.length === 1) return chemicals[0].chemical.color + 'CC';
   129   let r=0,g=0,b=0, tot=0;
   130   for (const c of chemicals) {
   131     const hex = c.chemical.color.replace('#','');
   132     r += parseInt(hex.slice(0,2),16) * c.volume;
   133     g += parseInt(hex.slice(2,4),16) * c.volume;
   134     b += parseInt(hex.slice(4,6),16) * c.volume;
   135     tot += c.volume;
   136   }
   137   if (tot === 0) return 'rgba(180,220,255,0.25)';
   138   const h = (n: number) => Math.min(255,Math.round(n/tot)).toString(16).padStart(2,'0');
   139   return `#${h(r)}${h(g)}${h(b)}CC`;
   140 }
   141 function mixPh(chemicals: VesselChemical[]): number {
   142   if (!chemicals.length) return 7;
   143   const tot = chemicals.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.volume,0);
   144   return tot ? chemicals.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.chemical.ph*c.volume,0)/tot : 7;
   145 }
   146 function phBarColor(ph: number): string {
   147   if (ph<=2) return '#EF4444'; if (ph<=5) return '#F97316';
   148   if (ph<=6) return '#EAB308'; if (ph<=8) return '#22C55E';
   149   if (ph<=10) return '#3B82F6'; return '#8B5CF6';
   150 }

   152 // ── SVG components ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   153 function BeakerSVG({ chemicals, isHeating, size=80 }: { chemicals: VesselChemical[]; isHeating: boolean; size?: number }) {
   154   const fill = blendColors(chemicals);
   155   const level = Math.min(1, chemicals.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.volume,0)/80);
   156   const W = size, H = size*1.1;
   157   const bodyX=W*0.12, bodyY=H*0.1, bodyW=W*0.76, bodyH=H*0.78;
   158   const liquidY = bodyY + bodyH*(1-level);
   159   const liquidH = bodyH*level;
   160   return (
   161     <svg width={W} height={H} viewBox={`0 0 ${W} ${H}`} style={{overflow:'visible'}}>
   162       <defs>
   163         <clipPath id={`bk-clip-${size}`}><rect x={bodyX} y={bodyY} width={bodyW} height={bodyH} rx="2"/></clipPath>
   164         <filter id="glass-blur"><feGaussianBlur stdDeviation="0.5"/></filter>
   165       </defs>
   166       {/* Shadow */}
   167       <ellipse cx={W/2} cy={H*0.95} rx={W*0.3} ry={3} fill="rgba(0,0,0,0.12)" />
   168       {/* Liquid */}
   169       {level>0 && <rect x={bodyX+1} y={liquidY} width={bodyW-2} height={liquidH}
   170         fill={fill} clipPath={`url(#bk-clip-${size})`} style={{transition:'all 0.5s ease'}}/>}
   171       {/* Shimmer */}
   172       {level>0 && <ellipse cx={W/2} cy={liquidY} rx={bodyW*0.45} ry={3}
   173         fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.35)" clipPath={`url(#bk-clip-${size})`}>
   174         {isHeating && <animate attributeName="ry" values="2;4;2" dur="0.9s" repeatCount="indefinite"/>}
   175       </ellipse>}
   176       {/* Bubbles when heating */}
   177       {isHeating && level>0 && [0.25,0.5,0.75].map((f,i)=>(
   178         <circle key={i} cx={bodyX+bodyW*f} cy={liquidY+8} r="2.5" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.55)">
   179           <animate attributeName="cy" values={`${liquidY+8};${liquidY-8}`} dur={`${0.6+i*0.18}s`} repeatCount="indefinite"/>
   180           <animate attributeName="opacity" values="0.7;0" dur={`${0.6+i*0.18}s`} repeatCount="indefinite"/>
   181         </circle>
   182       ))}
   183       {/* Glass body */}
   184       <rect x={bodyX} y={bodyY} width={bodyW} height={bodyH} rx="3"
   185         fill="rgba(220,240,255,0.10)" stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.85)" strokeWidth="1.8"/>
   186       {/* Glass highlight */}
   187       <rect x={bodyX+3} y={bodyY+4} width={3} height={bodyH-8} rx="1.5"
   188         fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.4)"/>
   189       {/* Lip */}
   190       <rect x={bodyX-3} y={bodyY} width={bodyW+6} height={5} rx="2.5"
   191         fill="rgba(191,219,254,0.8)" stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.7)" strokeWidth="1"/>
   192       {/* Scale ticks */}
   193       {[0.25,0.5,0.75].map((f,i)=>(
   194         <line key={i} x1={bodyX} y1={bodyY+bodyH*f} x2={bodyX+W*0.1} y2={bodyY+bodyH*f}
   195           stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.5)" strokeWidth="1"/>
   196       ))}
   197       {/* Spout */}
   198       <path d={`M ${bodyX+bodyW-4} ${bodyY} L ${bodyX+bodyW+6} ${bodyY-6}`}
   199         stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.8)" strokeWidth="2" fill="none" strokeLinecap="round"/>
   200       {/* Heat glow */}
   201       {isHeating && <rect x={bodyX} y={bodyY+bodyH-6} width={bodyW} height={6} rx="1"
   202         fill="#FCA5A5" opacity="0.6">
   203         <animate attributeName="opacity" values="0.3;0.8;0.3" dur="1.1s" repeatCount="indefinite"/>
   204       </rect>}
   205     </svg>
   206   );
   207 }

   321 function makeItem(kind: LabItem['kind'], x: number, y: number): LabItem {
   322   const labels: Record<LabItem['kind'], string> = {
   323     beaker:'Beaker', flask:'Flask', 'test-tube':'Test Tube', burette:'Burette',
   324     burner:'Bunsen Burner', stand:'Stand',
   325   };
   326   return { id: newId(), kind, x, y, chemicals:[], temperature:25, isHeating:false, label:`${labels[kind]} ${_id-100}` };
   327 }
   328 
   329 // ── Main component ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   330 export default function VirtualLabPage() {
   331   const { setScreen } = useApp();
   332 
   333   const [items, setItems] = useState<LabItem[]>([
   334     makeItem('beaker',     90, 180),
   335     makeItem('flask',     230, 190),
   336     makeItem('test-tube', 370, 200),
   337     makeItem('burner',    160, 310),
   338   ]);
   339   const [selected, setSelected]         = useState<string | null>(null);
   340   const [selectedReagent, setSelectedReagent] = useState<Chemical | null>(null);
   341   const [reactions, setReactions]       = useState<Reaction[]>([]);
   342   const [openCategory, setOpenCategory] = useState<string>('Acids');
   343   const [flameColor, setFlameColor]     = useState<string | undefined>(undefined);
   344 
   345   // Drag state — pure-ref approach: never call setItems on pointermove
   346   const dragRef  = useRef<{
   347     id: string;
   348     ox: number; oy: number;       // cursor offset from item origin
   349     sx: number; sy: number;       // pointer start position (to detect real drag vs click)
   350     moved: boolean;
   351   } | null>(null);
   352   const itemEls  = useRef<Record<string, HTMLDivElement | null>>({});  // DOM refs per item
   353   const posRef   = useRef<Record<string, { x: number; y: number }>>({});  // live positions
   354   const benchRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
   355 
   356   // Sync posRef whenever React state changes (initial mount + adds/removes)
   357   useEffect(() => {
   358     for (const item of items) {
   359       posRef.current[item.id] = { x: item.x, y: item.y };
   360     }
   361   }, [items]);
   362 
   363   const pushReaction = useCallback((rxn: Omit<Reaction,'ts'>) => {
   364     setReactions(r => [{ ...rxn, ts: Date.now() }, ...r].slice(0,10));
   365   }, []);
   366 
   367   // ── Pointer drag handlers — zero setState on move ─────────────────
   368   const onPointerDown = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent, id: string) => {
   369     if (e.button !== 0) return;
   370     e.preventDefault();
   371     e.stopPropagation();
   372     (e.target as Element).setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
   373     const el = itemEls.current[id];
   374     if (el) el.style.cursor = 'grabbing';
   375     const pos = posRef.current[id] ?? { x: 0, y: 0 };
   376     dragRef.current = {
   377       id,
   378       ox: e.clientX - pos.x,
   379       oy: e.clientY - pos.y,
   380       sx: e.clientX,
   381       sy: e.clientY,
   382       moved: false,
   383     };
   384   }, []);
   385 
   386   const onPointerMove = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
   387     const d = dragRef.current;
   388     if (!d || !benchRef.current) return;
   389     const dx = e.clientX - d.sx;
   390     const dy = e.clientY - d.sy;
   391     // Only start dragging after 6px movement — protects tap/click
   392     if (!d.moved && Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) < 6) return;
   393     d.moved = true;
   394 
   395     const rect = benchRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
   396     const nx = Math.max(0, Math.min(e.clientX - d.ox, rect.width  - 80));
   397     const ny = Math.max(0, Math.min(e.clientY - d.oy, rect.height - 100));
   398 
   399     // Move the DOM element directly — NO React setState → no re-render lag
   400     posRef.current[d.id] = { x: nx, y: ny };
   401     const el = itemEls.current[d.id];
   402     if (el) el.style.transform = `translate(${nx}px, ${ny}px)`;
   403   }, []);
   404 
   405   const onPointerUp = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent, id: string) => {
   406     const d = dragRef.current;
   407     dragRef.current = null;
   408     // Restore cursor immediately via DOM ref — no setState needed
   409     const el = itemEls.current[id];
   410     if (el) el.style.cursor = 'grab';
   411 
   412     if (!d || !d.moved) {
   413       // ── It was a TAP/CLICK — add reagent or select ──────────────
   414       if (selectedReagent) {
   415         setItems(prev => prev.map(it => {
   416           if (it.id !== id) return it;
   417           if (it.kind === 'burner' || it.kind === 'stand') return it;
   418           const chem = selectedReagent;
   419           const existing = it.chemicals.find(c => c.chemical.id === chem.id);
   420           let newChems: VesselChemical[];
   421           if (existing) {
   422             newChems = it.chemicals.map(c =>
   423               c.chemical.id === chem.id ? { ...c, volume: c.volume + 15 } : c
   424             );
   425           } else {
   426             newChems = [...it.chemicals, { chemical: chem, volume: 15 }];
   427             for (const ec of it.chemicals) {
   428               const rxn = findReaction(ec.chemical, chem);
   429               if (rxn) {
   430                 pushReaction({ text: rxn.text, color: rxn.color, effect: rxn.effect });
   431                 break;
   432               }
   433             }
   434             if (chem.type === 'metal-salt') {
   435               const flame = FLAME_COLOURS[chem.id];
   436               if (flame) {
   437                 pushReaction({ text: `🔥 Flame test: ${chem.name} → ${flame.name} flame`, color: flame.color, effect: 'flame' });
   438                 setFlameColor(flame.color);
   439               }
   440             }
   441           }
   442           return { ...it, chemicals: newChems };
   443         }));
   444         setSelectedReagent(null);
   445       } else {
   446         setSelected(prev => prev === id ? null : id);
   447       }
   448       return;
   449     }
   450 
   451     // ── It was a DRAG — commit final position to React state once ──
   452     const finalPos = posRef.current[id];
   453     if (finalPos) {
   454       // Reset transform (position is now baked into left/top via state)
   455       const el = itemEls.current[id];
   456       if (el) el.style.transform = '';
   457       setItems(prev => prev.map(it =>
   458         it.id === id ? { ...it, x: finalPos.x, y: finalPos.y } : it
   459       ));
   460     }
   461     e.preventDefault();
   462   }, [selectedReagent, pushReaction]);
   463 
   464   // Toggle burner
   465   const toggleBurner = (id: string) => {
   466     setItems(prev => prev.map(it => {
   467       if (it.id !== id) return it;
   468       const newOn = !it.burnerOn;
   469       if (newOn) {
   470         // Heat nearby vessels
   471         const burner = it;
   472         setTimeout(() => {
   473           setItems(cur => cur.map(v => {
   474             if (v.kind === 'burner' || v.kind === 'stand') return v;
   475             const dx = v.x - burner.x, dy = v.y - burner.y;
   476             if (Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy) < 120) {
   477               if (v.chemicals.length > 0) {
   478                 pushReaction({ text:`🔥 ${v.label} is heating — vapour rising!`, color:'#DC2626', effect:'none' });
   479               }
   480               return { ...v, isHeating: newOn, temperature: newOn ? 100 : 25 };
   481             }
   482             return v;
   483           }));
   484         }, 1500);
   485       }
   486       return { ...it, burnerOn: newOn };
   487     }));
   488   };
   489 
   490   const emptyItem = (id: string) =>
   491     setItems(prev => prev.map(it => it.id===id ? { ...it, chemicals:[], temperature:25, isHeating:false } : it));
   492   const removeItem = (id: string) => {
   493     setItems(prev => prev.filter(it => it.id!==id));
   494     if (selected===id) setSelected(null);
   495   };
   496   const addItem = (kind: LabItem['kind']) => {
   497     const rect = benchRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
   498     const cx = rect ? rect.width*0.4 + Math.random()*120 : 200;
   499     const cy = rect ? rect.height*0.3 + Math.random()*100 : 150;
   500     setItems(prev => [...prev, makeItem(kind, cx, cy)]);
   501   };
   502 
   503   const pour = (fromId: string, toId: string) => {
   504     if (fromId===toId) return;
   505     setItems(prev => {
   506       const from = prev.find(v=>v.id===fromId);
   507       const to   = prev.find(v=>v.id===toId);
   508       if (!from||!to) return prev;
   509       const totalVol = from.chemicals.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.volume,0);
   510       if (totalVol===0) return prev;
   511       const ratio = Math.min(1, 20/totalVol);
   512       // Check reactions
   513       for (const fc of from.chemicals) {
   514         for (const tc of to.chemicals) {
   515           const rxn = findReaction(fc.chemical, tc.chemical);
   516           if (rxn) { pushReaction({ text:rxn.text, color:rxn.color, effect:rxn.effect }); break; }
   517         }
   518       }
   519       return prev.map(v => {
   520         if (v.id===fromId) return { ...v, chemicals: v.chemicals.map(c=>({...c,volume:c.volume*(1-ratio)})).filter(c=>c.volume>0.5) };
   521         if (v.id===toId) {
   522           const merged = [...v.chemicals];
   523           for (const fc of from.chemicals) {
   524             const idx = merged.findIndex(m=>m.chemical.id===fc.chemical.id);
   525             if (idx>=0) merged[idx]={...merged[idx],volume:merged[idx].volume+fc.volume*ratio};
   526             else merged.push({chemical:fc.chemical,volume:fc.volume*ratio});
   527           }
   528           return { ...v, chemicals: merged };
   529         }
   530         return v;
   531       });
   532     });
   533   };
   534 
   535   // No isDragging state — cursor is updated via DOM ref to avoid any re-renders during drag
   536   const onBenchPointerMove = onPointerMove;
   537 
   538   const selectedItem = items.find(i => i.id === selected) ?? null;
   539   const vessels = items.filter(i=>i.kind!=='burner'&&i.kind!=='stand');
   540   const ph = selectedItem ? mixPh(selectedItem.chemicals) : 7;
   541 
   542   // ── Category grouping for reagent shelf ───────────────────────────
   543   const categories = Array.from(new Set(CHEMICALS.map(c=>c.category)));
   544 
   545   // ── Equipment rack items ───────────────────────────────────────────
   546   const EQUIPMENT: { kind: LabItem['kind']; label: string; emoji: string }[] = [
   547     { kind:'beaker',     label:'Beaker',      emoji:'🧪' },
   548     { kind:'flask',      label:'Flask',        emoji:'⚗️' },
   549     { kind:'test-tube',  label:'Test Tube',    emoji:'🔬' },
   550     { kind:'burner',     label:'Bunsen',       emoji:'🔥' },

const FLAME_COLOURS: Record<string, { color: string; name: string }> = {
  licl:  { color:'#EF4444', name:'Red'     },
  nacl2: { color:'#F59E0B', name:'Yellow'  },
  kcl:   { color:'#A78BFA', name:'Lilac'   },
  cucl2: { color:'#10B981', name:'Green'   },
  srcl2: { color:'#DC2626', name:'Crimson' },
};

function findReaction(a: Reagent, b: Reagent): RxnRule | null {
  for (const rule of REACTION_RULES) {
    const [r1, r2] = rule.ids;
    if ((a.id === r1 && b.id === r2) || (a.id === r2 && b.id === r1)) return rule;
  }
  return null;
}

// ── Colour helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function blendColors(reagents: VesselReagent[]): string {
  if (!reagents.length) return 'rgba(180,220,255,0.25)';
  if (reagents.length === 1) return reagents[0].reagent.color + 'CC';
  let r=0,g=0,b=0,tot=0;
  for (const c of reagents) {
    const hex = c.reagent.color.replace('#','');
    r += parseInt(hex.slice(0,2),16)*c.volume;
    g += parseInt(hex.slice(2,4),16)*c.volume;
    b += parseInt(hex.slice(4,6),16)*c.volume;
    tot += c.volume;
  }
  if (!tot) return 'rgba(180,220,255,0.25)';
  const h = (n: number) => Math.min(255,Math.round(n/tot)).toString(16).padStart(2,'0');
  return `#${h(r)}${h(g)}${h(b)}CC`;
}
function mixPh(reagents: VesselReagent[]): number {
  if (!reagents.length) return 7;
  const tot = reagents.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.volume,0);
  return tot ? reagents.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.reagent.ph*c.volume,0)/tot : 7;
}
function phBarColor(ph: number): string {
  if (ph<=2) return '#EF4444'; if (ph<=5) return '#F97316';
  if (ph<=6) return '#EAB308'; if (ph<=8) return '#22C55E';
  if (ph<=10) return '#3B82F6'; return '#8B5CF6';
}

// ── SVG components ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function BeakerSVG({ reagents, isHeating, size=80 }: { reagents: VesselReagent[]; isHeating: boolean; size?: number }) {
  const fill = blendColors(reagents);
  const level = Math.min(1, reagents.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.volume,0)/80);
  const W = size, H = size*1.1;
  const bodyX=W*0.12, bodyY=H*0.1, bodyW=W*0.76, bodyH=H*0.78;
  const liquidY = bodyY + bodyH*(1-level);
  const liquidH = bodyH*level;
  return (
    <svg width={W} height={H} viewBox={`0 0 ${W} ${H}`} style={{overflow:'visible'}}>
      <defs><clipPath id={`bk-clip-${size}`}><rect x={bodyX} y={bodyY} width={bodyW} height={bodyH} rx="2"/></clipPath></defs>
      <ellipse cx={W/2} cy={H*0.95} rx={W*0.3} ry={3} fill="rgba(0,0,0,0.12)" />
      {level>0 && <rect x={bodyX+1} y={liquidY} width={bodyW-2} height={liquidH}
        fill={fill} clipPath={`url(#bk-clip-${size})`} style={{transition:'all 0.5s ease'}}/>}
      {level>0 && <ellipse cx={W/2} cy={liquidY} rx={bodyW*0.45} ry={3}
        fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.35)" clipPath={`url(#bk-clip-${size})`}>
        {isHeating && <animate attributeName="ry" values="2;4;2" dur="0.9s" repeatCount="indefinite"/>}
      </ellipse>}
      {isHeating && level>0 && [0.25,0.5,0.75].map((f,i)=>(
        <circle key={i} cx={bodyX+bodyW*f} cy={liquidY+8} r="2.5" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.55)">
          <animate attributeName="cy" values={`${liquidY+8};${liquidY-8}`} dur={`${0.6+i*0.18}s`} repeatCount="indefinite"/>
          <animate attributeName="opacity" values="0.7;0" dur={`${0.6+i*0.18}s`} repeatCount="indefinite"/>
        </circle>
      ))}
      <rect x={bodyX} y={bodyY} width={bodyW} height={bodyH} rx="3"
        fill="rgba(220,240,255,0.10)" stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.85)" strokeWidth="1.8"/>
      <rect x={bodyX+3} y={bodyY+4} width={3} height={bodyH-8} rx="1.5"
        fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.4)"/>
      <rect x={bodyX-3} y={bodyY} width={bodyW+6} height={5} rx="2.5"
        fill="rgba(191,219,254,0.8)" stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.7)" strokeWidth="1"/>
      {[0.25,0.5,0.75].map((f,i)=>(
        <line key={i} x1={bodyX} y1={bodyY+bodyH*f} x2={bodyX+W*0.1} y2={bodyY+bodyH*f}
          stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.5)" strokeWidth="1"/>
      ))}
      <path d={`M ${bodyX+bodyW-4} ${bodyY} L ${bodyX+bodyW+6} ${bodyY-6}`}
        stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.8)" strokeWidth="2" fill="none" strokeLinecap="round"/>
      {isHeating && <rect x={bodyX} y={bodyY+bodyH-6} width={bodyW} height={6} rx="1"
        fill="#FCA5A5" opacity="0.6">
        <animate attributeName="opacity" values="0.3;0.8;0.3" dur="1.1s" repeatCount="indefinite"/>
      </rect>}
    </svg>
  );
}

  const fill = blendColors(reagents);
  const level = Math.min(1, reagents.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.volume,0)/70);
  return (
    <svg width="72" height="96" viewBox="0 0 72 96" style={{overflow:'visible'}}>
      <defs><clipPath id="flask-liq"><path d="M23 36 L6 72 Q3 88 36 88 Q69 88 66 72 L49 36Z"/></clipPath></defs>
      <ellipse cx="36" cy="92" rx="22" ry="3" fill="rgba(0,0,0,0.12)"/>
      {level>0 && <path d="M23 36 L6 72 Q3 88 36 88 Q69 88 66 72 L49 36Z"
        fill={fill} style={{transition:'all 0.5s'}} clipPath="url(#flask-liq)"/>}
      {level>0 && <ellipse cx="36" cy={88-52*level} rx="22" ry="3" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.3)" clipPath="url(#flask-liq)"/>}
      {isHeating && level>0 && [20,36,52].map((x,i)=>(
        <circle key={i} cx={x} cy={88-52*level} r="2" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.55)">
          <animate attributeName="cy" values={`${88-52*level};${88-52*level-12}`} dur={`${0.65+i*0.2}s`} repeatCount="indefinite"/>
          <animate attributeName="opacity" values="0.7;0" dur={`${0.65+i*0.2}s`} repeatCount="indefinite"/>
        </circle>
      ))}
      <rect x="23" y="4" width="26" height="34" rx="3" fill="rgba(220,240,255,0.10)" stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.85)" strokeWidth="1.8"/>
      <path d="M23 36 L6 72 Q3 88 36 88 Q69 88 66 72 L49 36Z" fill="rgba(220,240,255,0.10)" stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.85)" strokeWidth="1.8"/>
      <rect x="25" y="7" width="3" height="28" rx="1.5" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.4)"/>
      <rect x="20" y="2" width="32" height="6" rx="3" fill="rgba(191,219,254,0.8)" stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.7)" strokeWidth="1"/>
      {isHeating && <ellipse cx="36" cy="86" rx="20" ry="4" fill="#FCA5A5" opacity="0.55">
        <animate attributeName="opacity" values="0.3;0.7;0.3" dur="1.1s" repeatCount="indefinite"/>
      </ellipse>}
    </svg>
  );
}

function BuretteSVG({ reagents }: { reagents: VesselReagent[] }) {
  const fill = blendColors(reagents);
  const level = Math.min(1, reagents.reduce((s,c)=>s+c.volume,0)/60);
  return (
    <svg width="28" height="140" viewBox="0 0 28 140" style={{overflow:'visible'}}>

      <ellipse cx="14" cy="136" rx="5" ry="2" fill="rgba(0,0,0,0.15)"/>
      {/* Liquid */}
      {level>0 && <rect x="9" y={118-110*level} width="10" height={110*level}
        fill={fill} clipPath="url(#bur-liq)" style={{transition:'all 0.5s'}}/>}
      {/* Tube */}
      <rect x="8" y="8" width="12" height="110" rx="2"
        fill="rgba(220,240,255,0.10)" stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.85)" strokeWidth="1.5"/>
      {/* Graduation marks */}
      {[0.2,0.4,0.6,0.8].map((f,i)=>(
        <g key={i}>
          <line x1="8" y1={8+110*f} x2="14" y2={8+110*f} stroke="rgba(147,197,253,0.6)" strokeWidth="1"/>
          <text x="16" y={8+110*f+4} fontSize="6" fill="rgba(100,100,120,0.7)" fontFamily="Inter,sans-serif">{(f*50).toFixed(0)}</text>
        </g>
      ))}
      {/* Stopcock */}
      <rect x="5" y="118" width="18" height="7" rx="3.5" fill="#4B5563" stroke="#374151" strokeWidth="1"/>
      <rect x="11" y="115" width="6" height="4" rx="1" fill="#6B7280"/>
